A temporary proposal was made regarding what form the committee should use for official correspondence with the Provincial Government. It was resolved to use official letters. The meeting adjourned. The committee's proposed donation appeal, circular, and constitution are recorded below:

Solicitation for Repairing the Confucius Forest and Temple in Qufu (Whether to use this draft requires Dai Jitao's approval) 86

I humbly believe that the governance of Great Harmony originates from the legacy of Confucius's writings. The flourishing of morality is recorded in the Three Principles of the People. Our late Premier, looking to the past and opening up the future, his respect for Confucius is self-evident. The Qufu Forest and Temple are the source of our country's moral culture. The documents of the Si River and the Zhu River serve as evidence and are tied to the observation of Chinese and foreign people. Therefore, since the late Zhou Dynasty, for more than two thousand years, although they have frequently been burned down, construction and restoration were carried out immediately, and further expansion was carried out. The temple looked solemn, and the scale was fully prepared. This is not only important for the inheritance of ancient sites, but also for the perception of people's hearts. During the Qufu battle in the 19th year of the Republic of China, the war and fire destroyed all the ancestral halls. The tombs were also bombed. It turned the scenic spots into a wasteland. All Chinese and foreigners who traveled to this place were filled with emotion when they visited the temple and felt sadness when they saw the ritual objects. If it is allowed to be abandoned, how can we glorify the prosperous era and create a grand transformation? However, the project is huge and requires the preparation of large funds in order to restore the original appearance. The accumulation of a mountain cannot be accomplished by a single basket of soil, and the setting of tripods is easy with the efforts of everyone. In addition to the initial donation and promotion, I hope that all comrades will do their best to donate and contribute to this grand event. All donations should be stored in the Central Bank nearby. Once a certain amount is collected, workers and materials will be hired immediately, and people will be sent to supervise the restoration, and expand civilization. By building new pavilions, the beauty of the palace walls will be fully restored, and it will be able to comfort the admiration of the high mountains. Furthermore, it is heard that there is the sound of string and bamboo music, which is in line with the purpose of preserving cultural relics. I respectfully write a brief solicitation, waiting for your good news.

Donation Circular (To all gentlemen in the field) 87

Respectfully informing you that the Confucius Forest and Temple in Qufu are tied to the observation of Chinese and foreign people. They were unfortunately destroyed in last year's war. The forests and temples of Zhou, Yan, Si, and Meng are also incomplete and in need of repair. Telegrams have been sent to Commander-in-Chief Chiang and Deputy Commander Zhang, who have approved assistance in their completion. However, the project is huge and difficult to support alone. A circular has been sent to all sectors to initiate fundraising. I have always admired your eminence and your emphasis on Confucianism. A single call from you will be echoed by all mountains. I dare to ask you to contribute generously, and to collect every bit of support, so that thousands of years of cultural relics can be restored to their original appearance, and the spirits of the sages will truly rest in peace. In addition to the donation solicitation, I respectfully send this letter, wishing you peace and well-being. Qufu Confucius Temple Restoration Preparatory Committee

Important News Two

Kailuan Mines Declare a Go-Slow 89

Management Refuses to Improve Workers' Treatment

And Resumes Two Days of Shutdown per Week

Tianjin Correspondence: Last month, the workers of Kailuan Mines requested the mining bureau to increase wages and improve treatment. The most important condition was a wage increase of two dimes per worker and improvements in treatment, such as preparing sufficient materials, increasing the number of white holes, and providing all types of workers with equal treatment and wage increases. Coal bars should be issued to workers in the winter, etc., with four attached conditions. They also requested a solution at the same time. The mining bureau did not respond to the workers' demands and posted a notice on the 4th of this month, stating that railway transportation was difficult and that there was too much coal stored in the mines, announcing a two-day shutdown per week. The workers were extremely indignant that the mining authorities had not come to their senses, and decided that the five mines would simultaneously start a go-slow on the 11th. From 9:00 AM to 11:00 AM that morning, workers did not work. More than 40,000 workers from Majiagou, Linxi, Kaiping, Guye, and Tangshan mines participated. In order to maintain order, the trade union organized maintenance teams in each mine to supervise the workers' actions. Executive committee members of the trade union traveled to various mines to direct everything to avoid accidents. Therefore, the go-slow was well-ordered and there were no riots. The Public Security Bureau did not interfere. The steps to be taken for the go-slow have not yet been fully determined. Special Commissioner Wang Chaowen from the Central Party Headquarters arrived in Tangshan and gave a speech to the trade union committee at the Kailuan Mining General Trade Union, advising them not to be extreme and to wait for a solution. At the same time, he telegraphed the Central Party Headquarters to report the situation of the go-slow. The Kailuan Mining General Trade Union's declaration of the go-slow is recorded below: "Our association accepts the resolutions of the general meetings of the miners of each mine, and is scheduled to implement the go-slow on May 11. We are afraid that all sectors will not understand the truth, so we will separately state the stubborn and unreasonable actions of the mining bureau and the steps taken during the go-slow as follows. The workers' request for a wage increase and improved treatment is not without reason, nor is it an excessive demand. The entire benefit of it has been assessed in advance, and the benefits that the workers should receive have been fully calculated. The amount issued to workers by the mining bureau is less than one percent. Before submitting the conditions, we told and encouraged each other with the true meaning of labor-management cooperation. For fear that it would not be enough to awaken them, we cited clear examples of labor-management cooperation abroad in detail. In today's society, labor-management cooperation means mutual benefit and coexistence, otherwise both sides will lose, or even perish together. Therefore, if the mining bureau slightly considers the lives of workers, it will definitely respond generously to these conditions. However, after the conditions were submitted, the bureau initially used translation delays to shirk responsibility, then suppressed representatives from speaking during negotiations, and finally refused to attend mediation. Their contempt for the Chinese party and government and their oppression of hard-working workers can only be understood but not spoken of. Based on the above facts, the Kailuan workers can no longer endure it. We originally planned to use the last resort to shock the top, but because the party and government organs are still actively mediating, it is inconvenient to take extreme measures and there is room for change. Unexpectedly, on May 4, the mining bureau posted a notice stating that railway transportation was difficult and that there was too much coal stored in the mines, announcing a two-day shutdown per week. It is stated that no other actions are allowed during the mediation period, and the government has issued three orders and five applications. The workers can still be imprisoned and dare not violate it. The mining bureau is inching forward and treating the law as a mere formality, and openly announced the shutdown, which is clearly a provocation to us. The difficulty of transportation was caused by the road-mining dispute. Frankly speaking, it is their own fault. Why take it out on the workers? As for the excessive coal storage, it is even more absurd. During the military operations in the 17th year of the Republic of China, traffic was cut off, even for several months, and the coal storage in each mine reached hundreds of thousands of tons, but it did not lead to a shutdown. Now the transportation is not completely cut off, and the coal storage in each mine is less than two-tenths of what it used to be, but they are openly shutting down. Their intention is nothing more than to use the shutdown to threaten everything because of the road-mining dispute and the workers' conditions. Workers are in the autumn of rice and pearls and cinnamon, and are seeking to improve their lives. The mining bureau does not think about this, but instead takes further countermeasures, placing workers in a dangerous situation, in a situation of increasing heat in fire and deeper water. What's more, the workers have long been dissatisfied with the road-mining problem. They have long had the idea of supporting the railway. Now that the mining bureau has forced the workers into a dead end, it is difficult to expect the mining bureau to come to its senses without using the last resort. Therefore, it is scheduled to implement a go-slow by the Kailuan miners on May 11. During the go-slow, we dare to say that there will be no accidents. Special personnel are assigned to protect important work. After the go-slow, regarding the workers' livelihood problems, mining experts have been hired to survey the land near each mine for abundant ore deposits, and they will be mined on their own. The Beining Railway will be asked to provide transportation assistance. The workers' livelihood subsidies have been settled, and the order of the go-slow can be solemn. No matter how stubborn they are, they will eventually be made aware of it. However, in the autumn of wind and rain, it is time for us to help each other in the same boat. Although it is nominally a labor-management dispute, it is actually the struggle of the Chinese nation. We hope that all our compatriots will support it, which is our sincere hope. In addition to submitting it to the competent authorities for the record, we hereby declare it. Kailuan Mining General Trade Union, Tangshan, Hebei Province." (12th)

Anhui Province Establishes a Ship Management Office 90

Levying License Fees and Registration Fees

Foreign small steamers also levied temporary transit fees

Bengbu Correspondence: Chen Diaoyuan, Chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government, recently established the Anhui Provincial Ship Management Office to protect merchants. The Department of Civil Affairs commissioned to be the director of the office, and branch offices were established in various important places. Zhu Gongfu, director of the Bengbu branch, has arrived in Bengbu from the province and established a branch in the Yuelai Company in Hexia, preparing to levy ship license fees and registration fees. License registration is divided into four periods each year: January 1 to the end of March is the first period, April 1 to the end of June is the second period, July 1 to the end of September is the third period, and October 1 to the end of December is the fourth period. All ships sailing or stationed must apply to the ship management office or branch office for inspection and registration. They are allowed to pass after a license and registration number are issued. The method of collecting license and registration fees is based on the size of the ship's capacity, determining the amount of license fees to be collected. For example, those below 100 dan will be charged 2 jiao for the license fee and 2 jiao for the registration fee (hereinafter referred to as the license fee). Those above 100 dan and below 200 dan will be charged 8 jiao for the license fee and 4 jiao for the license fee. Those above 200 dan and below 300 dan will be charged 1 yuan for the license fee and 5 jiao for the license fee. Those above 300 dan and below 400 dan will be charged 1 yuan and 2 jiao for the license fee and 6 jiao for the license fee. Those above 400 dan and below 600 dan will be charged 1 yuan and 5 jiao for the license fee and 7 jiao for the license fee. Those above 600 dan and below 800 dan will be charged 2 yuan for the license fee and 8 jiao for the license fee. Those above 800 dan and below 1,000 dan will be charged 2 yuan and 5 jiao for the license fee and 1 yuan for the license fee. Those above 1,000 dan and below 1,500 dan will be charged 3 yuan for the license fee and 1 yuan and 2 jiao for the license fee. Those above 1,500 dan and below 2,000 dan will be charged 3 yuan and 5 jiao for the license fee and 1 yuan and 4 jiao for the license fee. Those above 2,500 dan and below 3,000 dan will be charged 4 yuan for the license fee and 1 yuan and 6 jiao for the license fee. Those above 3,500 dan and below 4,000 dan will be charged 5 yuan for the license fee and 2 yuan for the license fee. The license fee is collected in four periods each year, and the registration fee is collected once a year. The license fee for small steamers is 12 yuan per month, and the license fee for tugboats is 4 yuan per month. Licenses are exchanged monthly. The registration fee for small steamers and tugboats is 2 yuan each per year. All foreign small steamers passing through the Yangtze River or inland rivers in Anhui Province should obtain a temporary transit permit from the office, and the fee is 2 yuan each time. The license fee for fishing boats is 1 yuan per quarter, and licenses are exchanged quarterly. The license fee is 1 yuan per year, and licenses are exchanged annually, and must not be resisted. (May 13)

Harbin Navigation Association Issue Under Mediation 91

Navigation Association has agreed to concessions

Harbin Correspondence: After the Songhua River Shipping Merchants' Grand Union, merchants along the Songhua, Heilongjiang, and Wusuli rivers pointed out that the bureau has a monopolistic nature. Brokers also opposed it because they could not get freight rebates. This matter has been going on for a month now, and has not been completely resolved. Merchants downstream have jointly telegraphed the Jilin Provincial Government and the Northeast Political Affairs Committee, requesting that the bureau be abolished to avoid hindering the development of commerce in various places, and telegraphed the Binjiang City Chamber of Commerce to transfer the request to the Special Region Commander's Office to fight for it nearby. At the same time, they boycotted by stopping the transportation of goods. However, the Navigation Association still followed the plan and sent ships to upstream and downstream areas every day. However, due to the merchants' boycott of transportation, the ships only transported a small number of passengers. Officials believed that this long-term stalemate was hindering Binjiang's livelihood and commerce, and Harbin merchants were also deeply affected because merchants from various places did not come to purchase goods, so they repeatedly appealed to the authorities. Therefore, the Political Affairs Committee specially summoned Wang Shuncun, director of the official-merchant Navigation Association, to Liaoning at the end of last month to inquire about the matter, and ordered Wang to return to Harbin to find a solution. On the one hand, he telegraphed the Dong Province Special Zone Administrative Commander's Office to thoroughly investigate the truth and submit it for verification. Wang Shuncun returned to Harbin on May 6, and convened an emergency meeting of all directors and supervisors of the bureau on the afternoon of the 7th. It was resolved on the spot that in addition to people coming forward to mediate, a freight committee would be formed to discuss reducing freight by 15% to ease the momentum of the merchants. Recently, Binjiang Public Security Bureau Chief Gao Qilian, Binjiang County Chief Li Keyuan, and Commander's Office Finance Department Chief Song Ruxian have contacted the merchants. If a compromise can be reached, the Navigation Association is willing to suffer losses and make concessions. Representatives from the Fuyuan Yilan chambers of commerce and farmers' associations downstream have only exchanged letters and telegrams to negotiate opinions, and have not discussed concrete solutions for compromise. Therefore, after the Binjiang Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the mediator's opinion, they immediately telegraphed a reply, saying that before the 10th of this month, they would send representatives to Harbin to hold a meeting to discuss and decide. Therefore, whether this issue will expand depends on the arrival of representatives from various chambers of commerce and the outcome of their consultation. As for the Harbin ships, they currently only go to Fuyuan, Hurao, Heihe, and other places. The roads along the river are not safe and the ice floes have not been cleared. They must wait until May 15 to be able to navigate. (9th)

Jiangsu Province's Measures for Clearing Sand Fields 92

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance has formulated the Jiangsu Province's Measures for Clearing Sand Fields, which has been approved by the Provincial Government Conference, and is recorded as follows: (Article 1) Jiangsu Province will uniformly measure all sand fields in coastal counties along the river, except for those that have been transferred for shipping. (Article 2) The sand field area will be determined by the measurement team selected and sent by the Provincial Land Bureau to measure the triangular terrain, and the areas will be calculated separately for enclosed fields, grass beaches, and mud beaches. (Article 3) After the measurement of each sand field area is completed, a plan view should be drawn, and the Department of Finance will order the sand field sub-bureaus and the finance bureaus to bring the reed tax registers and measurement teams to check and measure the land house by house, verify the single documents and deed strings, and handle the method of paying prices and upgrading taxes separately. (Article 4) The sand field clearing fee is 2 jiao per mu for those with owners, and for those without owners, the sand field bureau will collect it together at the time of issuance according to the current regulations. (Article 4) The sand field sub-bureaus verify the evidence for the payment of prices and the compensation for becoming fields, and issue certificates for upgrading taxes. The finance bureau verifies the department's certificates, registers and registers, and issues printed documents. (Article 6) For sand fields that have been cultivated and matured, those who only paid beach prices in the past should pay the field price according to the number. Those who have property rights and have already transferred them to the buyer without a certificate to verify, they shall pay the beach price according to the department regulations. (Article 7) For the mu-fen of the measured overflow, the household that originally received the mu-fen should be ordered to apply for a certificate to make up for the value of the field and beach according to the department regulations within one month. If they do not receive it beyond the time limit, they will be divided out and sold. (Article 8) The measurement and release of newly risen beach land shall still be handled according to the value set by the department. (1) Those who have already enclosed and cultivated: (A) High-grade sand fields will pay 10 yuan per mu; (B) Medium-grade sand fields will pay 8 yuan per mu; (C) Low-grade sand fields will pay 6 yuan per mu, all to be paid in full at one time. (2) Those who have not been enclosed and cultivated: (A) High-grade grass beaches will pay 5 yuan per mu; (B) Medium-grade grass beaches will pay 4 yuan per mu; (C) Low-grade grass beaches will pay 3 yuan per mu. After they become fields in the future, they will still pay the same price as before. (Article 9) For beach land close to commercial ports, which is suitable for building land, the price should be determined according to the current value and not be included in the above three grades. (Article 10) After the sand field is upgraded, the Department of Finance will issue printed documents as a certificate for practicing tax payment. The printed document fee is 2 jiao per mu. (Article 11) All sand fields of public nature shall be handled in accordance with private property. (Article 12) Matters not specified in these measures shall be handled in accordance with the Regulations for Clearing Sand Fields in Jiangsu Province. (Article 13) These measures shall be implemented after being discussed, decided and promulgated by the Jiangsu Provincial Government Committee.

Wuhu Quick News 93

The Wuhu Public Security Bureau believes that the Spring Cleaning Movement Conference must be held as an example, and specially sent letters to various organs and groups today, setting the afternoon of May 15th at 2:00 PM to be held in the Big Garden. All sectors should bring their own flags and brooms to participate and form groups to parade and implement cleaning up garbage. The YMCA also plans to hold a fly-killing campaign at the same time, which is being actively prepared.

In recent years, counties in southern Anhui, such as Qingyang, Guangde, Nanling, and Dangtu, have promoted silkworm farming with considerable success. However, around the beginning of summer this year, there have been continuous rains and the weather has been suddenly cold and hot, which has greatly affected silkworms. Rapeseed and wheat have also been hit hard, and it is difficult to expect a good harvest.

The County Propaganda Department has set the week of May 22nd to launch a literacy campaign publicity week, with various lower-level party departments and schools responsible for publicity work.

The County Chamber of Commerce held a joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees today because various trade associations opposed the advertising donation. They all believed that Wuhu is not a city area, and there is no reason to collect advertising donations. It was resolved to send a letter to the Public Security Bureau to request that the donation be cancelled immediately.

The Wuhu Customs Department has now been reassigned by the General Tax Department to Japanese national Tsuda Toshitaro to succeed as the head. Tsuda came to Wuhu yesterday and took office at the customs today.

Duan Tianzhen, Commissioner of Construction in Wuhu County, is currently unable to implement various construction plans due to lack of funds, and has specially submitted his resignation to the Department of Construction. (12th)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 94

Record of the 4th Annual Meeting of Provincial People's Education Centers: The 4th Annual Meeting of Provincial People's Education Centers was held in Songjiang starting on the 13th. At the general meeting yesterday afternoon, the representatives from Songjiang Nan and Zhenjiang were nominated as the presidium, and it was resolved to rename it the Jiangsu Mass Education Society, and the articles of association were passed. More representatives arrived today, and 109 people attended the morning meeting. Zhao Guangtao, a representative from Nanjing, chaired the meeting, and more than 50 motions were passed. After the meeting, the group gathered in the square to take a photo. Because of the hygiene exhibition at this year's annual meeting, Jin Shishan, Director of the Ministry of Internal Affairs, and Yu Qingtang, Section Chief of the Department of Education, both came to the meeting to attend speeches. Director Jin also brought a lot of hygiene film dramas and publicity publications, which will be delivered at the auditorium of the First People's Education Center tonight, with the topic "Talking about the Importance of Public Health," and will show hygiene film dramas. Tomorrow (15th) morning, a general cleaning will be held, and a lantern parade will be held in the evening. Various groups have prepared various hygiene-related lanterns to promote the attention of the general public. It is truly a grand event. Awards were given at the primary and secondary school sports meet: The county's primary and secondary school sports meet was held for three days starting on the 11th. This afternoon at 4:00 PM, all competitions were completed. After the total scores were calculated by the recorders, the champion of the secondary school men's group was the County Middle School, which won four championships. The County Middle School also won three championships in the secondary school women's group. The champion of the primary school men's group was Public First School, and the champion of the women's group was reportedly Elementary School. The awards were given by the chairman of the meeting, Jin Qingzhang.

Suzhou 95

Establishment of the Reformatory: The Jiangsu Reformatory established by the High Court has been completed, and the internal layout has also been completed. Yesterday (14th), President Lin notified the assistants to send personnel to take turns to serve in it, and set June 1st to start work. All the counter-revolutionary criminals who have been convicted in various prisons have been ordered by the court to submit a list, and those who meet the reform regulations will be transferred to the Reformatory for reform.

Another hearing in the Lu Shiqiao murder case: Lu Shiqiao, a doctor in Beishang Township, Wuxi, was sentenced to death by the Wuxi County Government for gathering people to kill Tan Qixuan. Lu did not accept the judgment and appealed to the High Court. The case was heard by Judge Li of the Second Criminal Division of the High Court for half a year. The trial could not be concluded because the witnesses presented by Lu failed to appear in court. Yesterday (14th), another hearing was held, but it was not concluded because witnesses still needed to be summoned for questioning. The hearing was adjourned and will be retried at a later date.

Wujiang 96

Yesterday's hearing on the kidnapping case near Beichi: The family of Ni Chengquan in Zhuangtianshang, Beichi Town, in the county was kidnapped by bandits and took away his mother, younger brother, and maid. The next morning, the bandits released Ni's mother and ordered her to quickly prepare 20,000 yuan to contact them at the lake. After Ni's mother returned home, it was heard that someone had asked the bandits to reduce the ransom, and the bandits agreed to reduce it to 2,200 yuan. The Ni family prepared the ransom and went to the mountains in Huzhou to contact them. Unexpectedly, after the ransom was handed over to the bandits, the bandits only released the maid A Jin, and ordered the maid to inform them to quickly prepare 50,000 yuan to redeem them. Now the Ni family is extremely frightened because they cannot raise the money.

Wuxi 97

Final Arguments in the Case of Wife Murdered by Smothering: Huang Rongchu, a villager from the sixth district (Tianshang City), is accused of smothering his wife, Shen Qin Xian. The prosecutor's office has concluded its investigation and filed a public indictment with the criminal court of the same court. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, Judge Yang Jian issued summons to Shen Qin Xian's brother, Shen Arong, her mother, Shen Yao Shi, and Gao Zi Qing's wife, Gao Shen Shi, as witnesses. Huang Rongchu, who was in custody, was also brought in for the trial. Lawyer Zou Binghu was appointed as the defendant's pro bono counsel. After questioning Huang Rongchu, Gao Shen Shi, Shen Arong, and Shen Yao Shi individually, Prosecutor Zhou announced the purpose of the case, stating that the case had been thoroughly investigated and Huang Rongchu had confessed to smothering his wife. Therefore, he should be sentenced according to the second half of Article 282 of the Criminal Code. Lawyer Zou then stood up to defend, arguing that Huang Rongchu was provoked by righteous indignation, leading to his wife's death, and requested leniency under Article 286 of the Criminal Code. Judge Yang announced the end of the arguments, scheduled the verdict for next Monday, and ordered Huang Rongchu to be returned to custody. The others were dismissed.

Prosecutor Appeals Ferry Overload Case: The "Heng Yi" ferry of the Taili Company's Xihou route capsized in Nantang due to overloading, resulting in the drowning of ten passengers. The families of the deceased jointly filed a lawsuit. After the trial, Judge Yang Jian sentenced Yang Xiangqi to a fine of 500 yuan and Xiang Sanbao to four months in prison. Lu Xingsheng was acquitted. The civil lawsuit is being tried separately by the civil court. It is now known that Prosecutor Zhu Zonghai of the prosecutor's office has expressed dissatisfaction with the acquittal of Lu Xingsheng and filed an appeal with the High Court yesterday, in accordance with Article 375 of the Criminal Procedure Law.

Changzhou 98

Xuejiaqiao Security Corps Guns Robbed: The townsfolk of Xuejiaqiao, located about five li outside the Dabeimen in the fourth district of Wuyi County, had formed a security corps due to local unrest. The corps had eight members and eight rifles. Recently, as bandits were successively arrested and executed, the defense became lax. Unexpectedly, around 3:00 AM on the 13th, more than 20 bandits broke into the corps' headquarters while the members were asleep and stole all the guns. The corps leader immediately reported the robbery to the fourth district office, requesting that it be forwarded to the county government for the arrest of the escaped bandits and the recovery of the stolen guns.

Permission Granted to Open Coffin for Re-examination in Strange Death Case: In the case of a strange death of a man in Wujia Village near Luoyang Town in the sixth district of Wuyi County, Wu Canxing recently filed a petition with the county court, requesting that the coffin be opened for re-examination. The court session was held on the 13th. Sun Shi, Wu's nephew's wife, testified that her husband, Wu Fa, was at home on March 12 of the old calendar when she was picking mulberry leaves in the fields. When she returned, her husband was gone. When she asked the children at home, they said someone had called him away. He has been missing since that night and has not been seen. The photograph that was found was taken more than ten years ago and doesn't look very similar to him. However, according to rumors, he was beaten to death. Therefore, she is willing to make a statement requesting that the coffin be opened for re-examination. Based on the testimony, the judge ordered a visit to the village on the 15th to re-examine the case and determine the truth.

Jiangyin 99

Prisoner Accuses Guard of Smoking Opium: Zeng Guochen, a prison officer in this county, was transferred to Suzhou by order of the High Court. Zhang Zonglie, a prison officer from Songjiang, was appointed to replace him. Zhang took office on the 11th. Yesterday (the 12th), Yang Shengmei, a convicted prisoner from Wuxian County who was held in the third prison of Suzhou, reported to Zhang that the guard, Zhu Runqing, was smoking opium and produced opium paraphernalia. The matter was reported to the county in the afternoon and examined by Wu, the trial officer. Guard Zhu denied smoking opium, stating that the paraphernalia was found by the previous officer, Lu Ying, in the cell and placed under the bed. Yang Shengmei testified that Zhu smoked in the kitchen. An order was issued to investigate and verify the matter.

Impersonating Newspaper to Extort Police Chief: On the morning of the 12th, Wang Zuyin, the acting police chief of the first police station in the north city gate, received a phone call from someone claiming to be Xu from the Cheng Qing Daily of the county party headquarters. The caller said that a woman was detained the previous night with two packages of opium and the police chief released her after receiving a bribe. The caller said he could negotiate with the newspaper on the police chief's behalf to compensate the loss. Police Chief Wang, believing there was no such incident, was investigating when Gao Baosheng came to intercede. He was immediately detained and taken to the first precinct for questioning. Realizing his mistake, he begged for forgiveness. Director Cui of the precinct, considering the matter to be extortion, sent him to the headquarters to be interrogated by the county.

Danyang 100

Summary of Robberies in the Southeastern Countryside: At about 11:00 PM last night, more than ten robbers broke into the home of Chen Faling, a farmer in Machangli Village in the eastern countryside, by climbing over the wall and looting the house. Faling was unable to escape and was seized by the robbers, who demanded cash, causing a knife wound to his finger. Also last night, the home of Mao Changchun in Yaogan Village in the southern countryside was robbed by bandits. A farmhand resisted and was injured. The cases have been reported to the police for investigation and arrest.

Change of Trial Officer: Guan Liting, the trial officer of this county, has been dismissed from his post for exceeding his leave limit and transferred to the provincial government to await another appointment. He Bingzhou has been specially appointed to replace him and has arrived in Danyang yesterday to take office.

Zhenjiang 101

Appeal of Lawyer Zhou Fengyi Opens: Zhou Fengyi, a famous lawyer from Jiangdu, was previously accused of smoking opium and sentenced to one month in prison and a fine of 30 yuan. Zhou refused to accept the verdict and appealed in Zhenjiang. Yesterday, the criminal court judge, Yang, conducted the trial. Many lawyers attended the hearing. Zhou testified that he did not smoke opium and was dissatisfied with the hospital's examination results. The judge ordered him to pay an additional deposit of 150 yuan and await the verdict.

Provincial Government Replaces Six County Magistrates: Yesterday, the Provincial Government Committee held its 398th meeting. At the proposal of Hu, the committee member and Director of Civil Affairs, the county magistrates of Jiangyin and Donghai, among others, were removed. The details of the six counties are as follows: Wang Jiwu, the magistrate of Jingjiang County, was removed and replaced by Li Leng, the magistrate of Jiangyin County. Peng Guoyan, who passed the first county magistrate examination and was the former magistrate of Wuxian County, was appointed as the acting magistrate of Jiangyin County. Chen Baoqun, the magistrate of Gaochun County, was dismissed and replaced by Wang Guanxian, who passed the first county magistrate examination and was the former magistrate of Baoying and Funing counties. Zhou Juesheng, the magistrate of Qidong County, was dismissed and replaced by Fei Gongxia, the current inspector of the Department of Civil Affairs. Gong, the magistrate of Muyang County, was replaced by Shen Zhenjia, who passed the second county magistrate examination. Wu Jiandong, the magistrate of Donghai County, was dismissed and replaced by Zhang, a qualified county magistrate selected and recorded for future use.

Gaoyou 102

Case of Brother-in-Law Strangling Sister-in-Law: Disinterment and Examination of Bones: Xia Meizhu, a farmer from Xiajiaji in the tenth district of the county, and his father-in-law, Liu Hengyu, reported to the county government that Xia Meilian and others had strangled his wife, Xia Liu Shi. The examination began yesterday at the Qigong Temple. The coroner Guo took out the remains one by one and washed them clean. Due to the overcast sky, the examination could not be completed, so the remains were first placed in a small wooden box, sealed with a county government seal, and ordered the police to guard them together with the plaintiff and the defendant. This morning (the 12th) at 10:00 AM, County Magistrate Wang, Trial Officer Ji, and Coroner Guo arrived to examine the remains. First, the remains were steamed in a cage and then examined. The results showed that there were ten fewer upper teeth, and all the lower teeth were present, with five of them red. The cervical vertebrae were red. Both the upper and lower sections of the left arm bone were red. There was a bruise on the right radius, with a clear red blood mark. There was a scratch on the left radius, with a red blood mark. Five sections of the left fingers were red, and four sections of the right fingers were red. It was determined that the injuries were sustained before the death by hanging.

Pinghu 103

Restoration of Traffic on Shanping Bridge: Shanping Bridge, the border between this county and Jiashan County, was blocked with wooden stakes in the waterway by order of the military authorities at the Shuangxi Village Council due to rampant banditry. Although the area was temporarily at peace, transportation was greatly inconvenienced. Now that the bandits have been suppressed, the village council has received approval from higher authorities to restore water traffic in the area. The removal of the wooden stakes began on the 13th.

Silk Cocoon Tax Changed to Business Tax: The Pinghu County Business Tax Bureau received a telegram from the Department of Finance stating that the tax rate for the silk cocoon industry in the province's business tax rate table is set at two per thousand. The silk cocoons of this season are about to be on the market, and all county bureaus are ordered to verify and collect the tax according to the fixed rate. The silk cocoon tax of previous years has been completely abolished from this year onwards, in accordance with the national government's circular.

Ningbo 104

Yucheng Pawnshop in West Gate Burns Down: Yucheng Pawnshop in Gangqiao Lane, West Gate of Ningbo, has been in business for many years and has been quite prosperous. At 7:30 PM on the 12th, the storage building on the left side of the pawnshop, which stored wooden furniture and cotton quilts, suddenly caught fire for unknown reasons. The fire was very fierce, and firefighters from the city and suburbs rushed to the scene. Because the walls of the building were high, it was difficult to put out the fire. After more than an hour, the fire was extinguished. It is estimated that five buildings, more than a hundred cotton quilts, and wooden furniture were burned, totaling losses of over ten thousand yuan.

Xiaoshan 105

Bandits Rob Boats in Succession: Jingyou River in the southern countryside of Xiaoshan, is the main route from Linpu to Zhuji Paitou. Recently, bandits have been rampant in the area, and robberies of boats and goods have been frequently reported. On the night of the 9th of this month, two night boats and three cargo ships sailing from Zhuji to Linpu were forced to the shore by more than ten bandits and looted. The belongings of the nine passengers, including clothing and quilts, worth over a hundred yuan, were taken away. Unexpectedly, on the night of the 12th, a boat sailing from Paitou to Linpu was also robbed, with losses estimated at over two hundred yuan. The boat owners have reported to the water police and requested a search. In addition, night voyages have been suspended to prevent accidents.

Passenger Ship Sinks Sailing Boat, Request for Negotiation: Xu Dayu, a boat owner from Wutu Village in Xiaoshan, owned a "Xu Huiyuan" sailboat loaded with passengers and goods to be sold in the Min and Yue areas after sailing from Nantong Port. Unexpectedly, on the 5th of last month, the ship was sunk by the Japanese ship "Yijin Maru," causing a loss of 20,000 yuan. The boat owner has submitted a petition to the county executive committee, requesting that it be forwarded to the Central Executive Committee, which should then forward it to the foreign affairs authorities for serious negotiation.

Tragic News Amidst Poor Silkworm Farming: Due to continuous rain and a sudden drop in temperature, the silkworm farming in the four townships has been severely affected. The poor silkworm farming in Shantou Peng, Xiaosipu, and other places is unprecedented in recent years. Eight or nine out of ten families have given up. On the 12th, two sisters-in-law named Xu, farmers in Shadi, jointly raised more than two liang of silkworm eggs and ordered mulberry leaves worth 48 yuan. Unexpectedly, after the third sleep, they completely vomited yellow water and died. The two women were devastated by this blow and had no source of income for silkworm farming, resulting in debts of dozens of yuan. Overcome with remorse, the two women suddenly had a suicidal thought. In the middle of the night, each of them took brine to end their lives. The next morning, they were discovered by their neighbors, who tried to save them in every way. One woman died due to the deep poisoning, while the other woman was fortunate to have taken less poison and is not in danger of death.

Xuyi 106

Capture of Red Bandit Zhang Pengchao and Others: Xuyi is located on the border of northern Anhui, surrounded by mountains and beaches. Bandits have been rampant. In recent years, troops have come and gone, and bandits have come and gone, causing disasters that have been reported in various newspapers. Recently, red bandits have infiltrated the territory again and colluded with local bandits. Fortunately, heavy troops were sent to suppress them, and peace has finally been restored. Zhang Pengchao (also known as Bo Fei or Bai Fei), Wu Jingxiu, Hua Kaihao, and other leaders of the red bandits who were active in Xuyi have been secretly ordered to be arrested by the Anhui Provincial Government, but they have not been captured. Now, the two key criminals, Wu Jingxiu and Hua Kaihao, were arrested last month. County Magistrate Jiang Shuxun welcomed them back to the county a few days ago. The provincial government has telegraphed to have them escorted to the province for legal action. Recently, the people of the county have organized a communist eradication group and issued a declaration, detailing the disasters caused by the red bandits Wu Jingxiu and others in Xuyi, hoping that all the people of the county will rise up together to eliminate them.

Letter Received

Letter from the Secretariat of the Ministry of Railways 107

Dear Editor,

In the Capital News column of your newspaper on the 13th, there is a statement that "Vice Minister Huang Hanliang of the Ministry of Railways telegraphed to Beijing to move his family, and Vice Minister Lian Sheng Hai is currently on sick leave and replaced by Counselor Guan Genglin." After investigation, the statement is inconsistent with the facts. Vice Minister Huang of this ministry did not telegraph to Beijing to move his family. Vice Minister Lian did occasionally suffer from illness, but he still worked diligently and did not take leave. The statement "replaced by Counselor Guan Genglin" is even more fictitious. I am writing to request that your newspaper promptly correct the statement.

Sincerely,

Secretariat of the Ministry of Railways

May 13th

Education News

Fifth Jiangnan University Sports Meet Opens Today

——Seven Schools Participating, Including Female Athletes This Year——

——Venue at Guanghua, East China Athletes Compete——

The fifth track and field meet of the Jiangnan University Sports Association, as decided by the executive committee, is scheduled to be held today and tomorrow at Guanghua University on Daxi Road. Guanghua, as the host, is responsible for the preparations, and everything is generally ready. The opening ceremony will be held formally at 1:30 PM today. Seven schools are participating: Central University, Jinan University, Daxia University, Guanghua University, Fudan University, Jiaotong University, and China Public School. Chi Zhi University is also a member, but it is regrettable that they are not participating in the most important track and field events. This year's competition will have two championships, one for field events and one for track events. The 3,000-meter race has been canceled and replaced with a 10,000-meter race. The 200-meter low hurdles have been changed to 400-meter intermediate hurdles, and the 12-pound shot put has been changed to 16 pounds. In short, the competition will be conducted entirely according to Far Eastern rules. A women's division has also been added, which is unprecedented. In addition, anticipating that preparatory students will not be able to participate in the championship competition, an open division has been specially set up for preparatory students to compete. The intention is excellent. Generally speaking, most of the athletes from the seven schools are outstanding talents from East China, and the Jiangnan University Sports Association is also the largest sports organization in East China. It is expected that this competition will produce good results. However, due to the heavy rain last night, the track is soft, which may affect the track event results. If there is heavy rain today, the competition will be postponed. If there is light rain, the competition will proceed as scheduled. The details are as follows:

Venue Arrangement 108

The sports field was recently built, and the track is slightly soft. The perimeter is 400 meters. The starting points for the 100-meter, 50-meter, and hurdles are in the southwest corner of the field. Next to it is the rostrum, with a press box on top. The finish line for middle and long-distance races is near the starting point for the 100-meter race. The starting point for the 200-meter race is in the northeast corner of the field. In front of the university classroom, an additional 60-foot grandstand from the China Baseball Field has been borrowed and installed next to the 100-meter starting point, which is also the finish line for middle and long-distance races, so that spectators can sit and watch. The long jump is in the west of the field, the high jump and javelin throw are in the south of the field, the pole vault pit is in the east of the field, the shot put is in the northeast corner, and the discus is in the northwest corner. The overall arrangement of the field is quite organized.

Directions to the Venue 109

Guanghua University is located in western Shanghai, far from the bustling center. Those coming from outside the area can follow the directions below: (1) Take a trolley or bus to Jing'an Temple, get off at Jing'an Temple, and then take a rickshaw to the school. The rickshaw fare is about 30 to 35 cents. (2) Take a rickshaw directly from Zhaofeng Garden. The fare is about 20 cents. (3) Take the Xujiahui tram to Fucaixin Road, and then take a rickshaw for about 20 cents to reach the venue. In addition, there is a Guanghua University bus at the intersection of Sanma Road and Yunnan Road (in front of Moore Memorial Church), waiting at any time. The fare is also 20 cents.

(1) Jiangnan University Officials: Honorary President Zhang Shouyong, President Shi Ying, Vice President Shen Guoquan, Secretary Wu Yanzhang.

(2) Executive Committee: Chairman Wang, Chairman Wang Fudan, Secretariat Xue Dijing, Venue Jiang Jingnan, Competition Lu Xiangqian.

Strength Assessment 113

Central University: Central University was the champion of the previous meet. This year, they have abundant talent, with the largest team of the seven schools, totaling 30 people. Among them, the previous winners, such as Chen Ling, Zhao Rugong, and Zhang Yuansheng, are still on the roster this year. Chen Ling's hurdles performance this year has improved to 16.9 seconds, which is the most stable. His high jump of 1.718 meters will compete with Fudan's Li Lin for the top spot. Zhao Rugong's highest long jump score is 6.71 meters, and he has the most hope. He can score in the triple jump. Zhang Yuansheng's 1500-meter race has improved to 4 minutes 42.9 seconds, and he will also compete with Ma Fengrui. He may also score in the 800-meter race.

China Public School: Ma Fengrui is highly anticipated. Everyone knows about his long-distance running. His 34 minutes 12.5 seconds in the 10,000-meter race, 4 minutes 38.2 seconds in the 1500-meter race, and 2 minutes 10 seconds in the 800-meter race are outstanding. The top spot almost certainly belongs to him. Everyone hopes to see a new record.

Jiaotong University: Dai Ming is the king of the triathlon, but he has recently injured his foot, and it is still unknown whether his performance will be affected. If he does not work hard, Jiaotong University may have little hope.

Guanghua University: Wang Jizhun is the king of the field events. He will definitely win first place in the javelin throw. He had a special score of 46.94 meters at this school. He will compete with Central University's Zhao Rugong in the long jump, competing against Bai Hong with a score of 6.28 meters. His triple jump of 12.78 meters is also outstanding. He has a lot of hope in the 31.93-meter discus throw. Shu Zhaoxian can also score in the meet.

Fudan University: Abundant talent. Gu Zaiping's 11.2 seconds in the 100-meter race and 24 seconds in the 200-meter race are rare. Li Lin's 1.69-meter high jump and 3-meter pole vault will compete with Cao Yu and Chen Ling. His 1.69-meter high jump can only be challenged by Chen Ling.

Jinan University: The team is no less than Central University's. Zhong Lianji has just recovered from an illness, and it is doubtful whether he can recover his pre-illness performance. Hao Chunde and Huang Feilong may take a place in the sprints. Wen Dingxin's 42.75-meter javelin throw, although not as good as Wang Jihai, is a sure score. Xie Quanhe may get a position in the triathlon.

Daxia University: Daxia has a lot of talent, but He Debao, Long Zexian, and Chen Baoqiu are limited by the rules due to their freshmen status. However, Wu Jinqi's 6.23-meter long jump is sure to score.

Other Matters 114

Collect Number Cloths: Number cloths for male and female athletes will be issued this morning. It is hoped that each member will send someone to Guanghua to collect them.

Scoring Method: The top four finishers in each event will be awarded points, calculated as 5, 3, 2, 1. The women's relay race points are doubled, calculated as 16, 4, 2. The open division will not be scored and will not have a championship.

All-Around Competition: The men's five-event, ten-event, and relay races are collectively referred to as the all-around competition. It used to be mixed with the track and field meet, but it has been separated from this year onwards. It is heard that the all-around competition will be held around September or October.

Welcome to Central University: The Central University team arrived in Shanghai a few days ago and is staying at the Guanghua Middle School. Last night at 7:00 PM, Guanghua held a special welcome reception to promote the friendship between the two schools.

The Chinese Youth Basketball Tournament Successfully Concludes, White Emperor Wins the Championship 115

Thirty-seven to Thirty Victory Over Merchant Marine

The Chinese Youth Basketball Association has been running for two and a half months, holding a total of 176 games. Forty-seven teams participated, divided into six groups, competing for the championship. The sportsmanship of each team was excellent, and the results were commendable. Yesterday at 5 PM, White Emperor and Merchant Marine competed for the championship. After a fierce battle, White Emperor won with a score of thirty-seven to thirty, claiming the association's championship. The team has sent letters to the champions of each group, inviting them to an award ceremony and photo session this Saturday at 2 PM to commemorate the event.

A Chronicle of the Two Heroes' Battle for Supremacy

As the fifth bell rang and referee Chen Fuzhang's whistle sounded, the peaceful atmosphere was broken, and the athletes from both teams began their contest. Merchant Marine scored first, eliciting cheers from their supporters. White Emperor quickly caught up and regained the lead. From then on, the two teams were evenly matched, making it difficult to distinguish their strengths. Merchant Marine took the lead with a free throw, ending the first half with a score of eleven to ten. As the second half began, Merchant Marine launched a swift attack, scoring a long shot, greatly increasing their momentum. However, the White Emperor team remained calm and gradually recovered. Seizing an opportunity, they surged ahead, scoring ten consecutive points in five minutes, turning defeat into victory. Afterwards, Merchant Marine tried hard to catch up, but ultimately failed. As the game ended, White Emperor won with a score of thirty-seven to thirty.

Liaoning Track and Field Preliminary for the North China Games 116

Dongda's Zhao Lingzhi Sets National Javelin Record

Ma Zijun Breaks National Women's Shot Put Record

(Shenyang Correspondent) The Liaoning Province preliminary track and field meet for the North China Games was held at the Xueliang Sports Field on the 9th and 10th. The first day was originally scheduled to begin at 9 AM, but the javelins for the field events did not arrive in time, delaying the start until after 10 AM. President Feng Yong personally flew his Bili aircraft over the sports field several times to celebrate before the opening ceremony. After the competition began, it suddenly rained before several events were completed. However, the officials and athletes continued as planned. The second day was clear and bright, and the enthusiasm of the spectators was several times greater than on the first day. In terms of the competition results, there were no significant advantages or disadvantages among the men's teams. However, Zhao Lingzhi of Northeastern University set a new national javelin record with a throw of 46 meters (previous record 45.90 meters). The athletes from Antung County Girls' Middle School performed best in the women's division, especially Ma Zijun, whose 8-pound shot put set a new national record with a distance of 9.46 meters. The school won championships in every event they participated in. Their performance was even better than at last year's Northeast Four Provinces Joint Games. The Provincial Women's Normal School also showed considerable improvement. The gradual development of women's sports in Liaoning Province is evident from this. Liu Changchun did not participate in the men's senior division 100-meter and 200-meter races due to a leg injury sustained several days ago and is currently recovering. Xiao Dinghua also did not compete in the high hurdles due to a leg injury. In the 10,000-meter long-distance race on the second day, Liu Guxue of Northeastern University was expected to win and achieve the best record. However, after completing the seventh lap, he tripped and fell. After getting up and running several more laps, he was unable to finish the race due to the setback. The detailed results for both days are listed below:

Important News

Supplementary Measures for County Education Funds After Returning to the Finance Bureau 117

The Ministry of Education has approved the Ministry of Finance's reply regarding the supplementary measures for the resolution of the Internal Affairs Conference on the unified management of county local education funds by the Finance Bureau. A circular has been issued for compliance. A circular has been sent to the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities, stating that the Shandong Provincial Department of Education submitted a request for instructions regarding the Yunnan Provincial Government's proposal at the Internal Affairs Conference that county local education construction, police, and various expenses should be uniformly managed by the Finance Bureau. The request detailed the difficulties in implementing the proposal. The Ministry has consulted with the Ministry of Interior and drafted supplementary measures, which have been submitted to the Ministry of Finance for review and distribution for compliance. The Ministry of Finance has replied that the aforementioned measures have been circulated to the finance departments of all provinces and the finance bureaus of all cities for compliance. Therefore, in addition to separate orders, the original consultation is copied and sent to the said department for compliance and distribution for compliance by its subordinates.

Supporting the Declaration to Abolish Unequal Treaties 119

The Taxpayers' Association Cables the National Assembly Yesterday

The Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers Association cabled the National Assembly in Nanjing yesterday, stating: "To the esteemed National Assembly in Nanjing, our country has long suffered from the constraints of unequal treaties, which have undermined our sovereignty, ravaged our territory, fragmented our laws, invaded our economy, incited internal strife, and depressed the spirit of our nation, people's rights, and livelihood. Since the founding of the Republic of China by Dr. Sun Yat-sen, who called for the awakening of the people and led the National Revolution for forty years, the political situation in our country has undergone a transformation, and the world has taken on a new look. Dr. Sun's last will specifically called for the abolition of unequal treaties and the realization of this goal in the shortest possible time. Now that the country has been unified, the National Government, in accordance with Dr. Sun's will, is convening the National Assembly in the capital. All of you are representatives of the people of the whole country, upholding the legacy of the Premier, in addition to formulating the Provisional Constitution for the period of political tutelage, you should also realize the abolition of unequal treaties, issue a solemn declaration, and announce it to the world. Our association, as a group of Chinese people in the Shanghai International Settlement, has suffered the most severely from the pain of unequal treaties. We are willing to unanimously support the declaration to abolish the treaties, and we will not hesitate to overcome any difficulties and sacrifices in order to implement it. This telegram is respectfully submitted for your consideration. Respectfully, Wang Xiaolai and Xu Jiqing, Chairman of the Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers Association."

Cold Print,

Hygiene Week Campaign 120

Begins Today

The seventh Shanghai Hygiene Week campaign begins today. News about the posting of cholera prevention slogans and the implementation of work is detailed below:

Post Slogans The various slogans for this Hygiene Week were posted yesterday by the Municipal Health Bureau, which dispatched staff to major roads in the north and south of the city to post various slogans and charts, informing citizens about the dangers of cholera, methods of prevention, attention to hygiene, and vaccination. The bureau also sent staff to the cabins of buses, trams, and long-distance buses to post the slogans. Due to the vast territory of the city, it is planned to complete the posting of over 40,000 large and small slogans within the three days of the 14th, 15th, and 16th. The bureau instructed the Shanghai Rickshaw Association to supervise each rickshaw company to complete the posting of 40,000 small hygiene campaign slogans on rickshaws within the three days of yesterday (14th), today (15th), and tomorrow (16th). As for the publicity work in various rural areas of Shanghai, the bureau has informed the municipal commissioners of each rural area to post slogans and charts on behalf of the bureau and send staff to administer vaccinations.

Send Doctors for Vaccinations From today until the 21st,

the Municipal Health Bureau will send many doctors to various factories in the city to persuade factory workers to get vaccinated, with particular emphasis on encouraging the poor people in the city to get cholera vaccinations in order to prevent the spread of cholera. Organizations, institutions, and individuals with more than 30 people can directly notify the bureau, which will arrange for doctors to visit and administer vaccinations on a specific date. Individual citizens can go to the bureau for vaccinations during office hours, even outside the campaign week, at any time.

School Hygiene School hygiene administration has always been handled by the School Hygiene Section of the Municipal Health Bureau's Fourth Division. During this campaign week, the section will send a bundle of hygiene slogans and charts to each municipal school in the city for the school authorities to post. Doctors designated by the section will administer vaccinations to all students in municipal schools.

Vaccination Hospitals For the convenience of citizens, the Municipal Health Bureau has prepared a large number of smallpox vaccines and various preventive vaccines, which will be distributed to public and private hospitals and clinics in the north and south of the city. Citizens can go to the following hospitals to get vaccinated against cholera free of charge during the Hygiene Week and on weekdays from Monday to Saturday, 2 PM to 4 PM, according to the Municipal Health Bureau's announcement. The names of the hospitals are as follows: Shanghai Public Hospital, located on Duojia Road (i.e., Sanda Pier in Dongjiadu); Southeast Hospital, Xinhuying Xinpu Yutang; Nanshi Emergency Epidemic Hospital, Guohuo Road; Nanshi Poor People's Clinic, Dawang Temple Street; Waterside Pavilion Clinic, Xiaonanmen Waterside Pavilion; Zhonghua Hospital, Zhonghua Road, Xiaonanmen; Nanyang Hospital, East Huangjia Que Road; Women and Children's Hospital, Hongfangzi on Fangxie Road; Xinpu Yutang Zhabei Clinic, Baoshan Road; Ansheng Hospital, Baoshan Road West Baotong Road; Jisheng Hospital, No. 28 Baoshan Road; Lianhua Western Medicine Clinic, North Railway Station North Wangjiazhai; Pushan Hospital, Xinmin Road; Lianqingshe Children's Clinic (details not specified); Zhabei Clinic, Minli Road; Pudong Hospital, Lan Ni Du, Pudong; Pingmin Hospital, Xinjiang Road; Zhongde Hospital, Zhangjiabang, Racecourse, British Concession; Shanghai Labor Hospital, Xiaoshadu Road; Yimiao Medical Clinic, Chenghuangmiao Xingxiu Hall; Epidemic Hospital, Xizang Road.

Letter to Citizens Hu Hongji's Seventh Hygiene Campaign Letter to Citizens says,

Citizens, this is the seventh time that the city has held a hygiene campaign. In each campaign, the Health Bureau has distributed many important points of hygiene knowledge to citizens in the form of leaflets and slogans, or through announcements and advertisements, all in order to make everyone understand the true meaning of hygiene, gain more knowledge to protect their health, and become a citizen who knows how to pay attention to hygiene, and a healthy and promising national. Then, with the cooperative efforts of everyone, we can promote the overall public health cause, create a healthy nation, and wash away the shame of being the "sick man of East Asia." This is the purpose of our repeated appeals to citizens in each campaign. From various perspectives, we have observed that citizens of this city are now more aware of hygiene and have gradually paid attention to the importance of the relationship between hygiene and life. In the past two years, we have received more documents from citizens requesting the elimination of matters that harm hygiene, which shows the progress of citizens' public health knowledge. This is also something that the administrative organs in charge of hygiene are very pleased about, and it also makes us feel that our responsibility is great, and we must work hard to promote it. Because there are still many facts that tell us that a small number of citizens still have a weak understanding of public health knowledge and do not pay attention to the importance of public health. Let us take the prevention of cholera as an example. Everyone knows that cholera is a serious infectious disease that is most likely to occur every summer. The first method of prevention is to get vaccinated, and the second is to pay attention to diet. The more people who get vaccinated, the better, because a small number of people who do not get vaccinated still have a greater chance of being infected with cholera. Therefore, since its establishment, this bureau has paid special attention to prevention work, striving to make it universal. Every summer, we send many doctors to various places to give citizens free vaccinations. We send doctors to all public groups, schools, institutions, and factories with a large number of workers to give vaccinations. According to our experience over the years, there are indeed many citizens who actively accept vaccinations, but there are still some leaders or partners of organizations, factories, and shops who do not understand the benefits of cholera vaccination and refuse to get vaccinated. Sometimes, they even openly refuse. We speculate that their reasons for refusing to get vaccinated are nothing more than the following: (1) They think that going to get vaccinated while working will take up some working time; (2) They fundamentally lack public health knowledge and think that there is no need to get vaccinated if they are not sick. Aside from these two reasons, we cannot think of any other reasons for their refusal to get vaccinated. Because we send doctors out to give vaccinations completely free of charge, no matter where we go. The people who get vaccinated not only do not suffer any loss, but can also add to their body's ability to resist cholera. Why would they refuse to get vaccinated? Speaking of the first reason for refusing to get vaccinated, we dare to assert that it is entirely the private opinion of a few ignorant factory owners or employees, because their purpose is only to make a profit, and they think that if workers stop working for a while, the factory will suffer losses. This kind of mentality can be said to be very wrong. It not only shows that their selfishness is too heavy and their moral heart is too thin, but it can simply be said that they do not understand the principles of operating industrial and commercial enterprises in the current era. Because cholera is a highly infectious disease that is most likely to spread, and factories and shops are places with many people and complicated affairs, and there are many interactions between them, there is a greater chance of epidemic diseases spreading. Once cholera and other infectious diseases occur, there is a great danger of affecting the entire population. Therefore, preventing the occurrence of serious infectious diseases is to maintain the working ability of the partners. Hongji takes this opportunity to explain this principle, hoping that all the leaders and managers of factories and shops in the city will think about it more, and clearly and thoroughly recognize the direction they should take. Speaking of the second reason for refusing to get vaccinated, which we speculated earlier, it is entirely due to stubborn thinking and a lack of modern hygiene knowledge. They still regard infectious diseases as natural disasters and divine misfortunes, and do not know that cholera is entirely due to infection. Because it is extremely easy to transmit, it often kills many people in summer and autumn. Shanghai used to not pay attention to prevention, which led to cholera becoming a great scourge. There was a shocking fact that coffins were sold out. Citizens who have lived in Shanghai for many years must still remember it. Since this disease is so easy to transmit, even if people are currently healthy, they may immediately be infected through food, drink, or contact. Getting sick and suffering is a small matter, but their lives are in danger in an instant, and it may be too late to save them by seeing a doctor. Therefore, only by getting vaccinated can they add some resistance to their body, even if they are invaded and develop cholera, they can also reduce the severity of the disease and make it easier to cure. Therefore, getting vaccinated is an important method for everyone to prevent the harm of cholera and to protect their lives in summer and autumn. It is really wrong to say that there is no need to get vaccinated if they do not have cholera. As for paying attention to diet, it is also very important. Because cholera is entirely due to cholera bacteria causing problems in the intestines and stomach, people who get the disease vomit and have diarrhea. Therefore, we must be especially careful about what we eat and drink, especially not to eat raw water and things made with raw water, sprinkled with raw water, or things that flies have touched, because raw water and things that flies have touched often have cholera bacteria attached to them that cannot be seen by the naked eye. If they are mistakenly eaten and transmitted to the intestines and stomach, the bacteria will multiply and take people's lives. The Health Bureau has repeatedly announced this matter in the summer of the year, urging citizens to pay attention to it. However, according to our observations, citizens still lack special attention. This is something that we hope citizens in this city will improve starting this year. At the time when this Hygiene Campaign is being held, the Health Bureau is already carrying out the prevention of cholera this year. I hope that this year, all citizens will pay attention to prevention, get vaccinated, get rid of all unreasonable prejudices, encourage each other, and work hard together to reduce the harm of all epidemic diseases year by year, and to increase the level of citizens' hygiene knowledge year by year, so that future Hygiene Campaigns may not have to be held, and future hygiene agencies will only have to perform executive tasks for citizens, without having to do any more publicity and advocacy work. To realize the high level of Shanghai citizens in the new China, this is also something that Hongji sincerely hopes for on this occasion. Let us encourage each other and look forward to success together.

To Resolve the Current Social Panic Regarding Employment

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce sent letters to various industry associations and guilds yesterday, stating: "We are writing to you regarding a letter received from the China Vocational Education Society on the 11th of this month. The letter states that the backwardness of social production and the increasing impoverishment of the national livelihood are the greatest dangers facing China today. The Ministry of Education, recognizing this, issued a clear order in March of this year to promote vocational education. For more than a decade, our society has been working hard to research this matter, and only now has it gained the sympathy of society and the promotion of the government, which fulfills our private wishes. However, running vocational education is extremely difficult, with a myriad of details. In short, if we try to make education vocationalized, the results will be less effective. This is why vocational schools in various places, after being established for more than a decade, have not shown significant results. If we can make vocational education educationalized, the results will be more effective. This is why vocational education in various countries has been effective. Making education vocationalized inevitably creates some separation, while making vocational education educationalized allows for the benefit of matching supply and demand. Today, we hear of the suffering of unemployment while lamenting the lack of talent. This contradiction is clear evidence of the lack of communication between education and occupation. Although some vocational school graduates may not fully meet the needs, we believe that the best method is for each industry to establish its own specialized vocational school according to its needs. For example, major factories and shops in Europe, America, and Japan either run their own training centers or entrust educational institutions to handle appropriate materials. This is the intention behind this. Recently, various industries in Liaoning and Shenyang have also established vocational courses. Their meticulous planning and long-term vision are truly admirable. Shanghai is China's only major trading port, and each industry has a considerable organization. The leaders are all outstanding talents, admired by the national business community. If you can take the lead in advocating, it will surely move the attention of the world. Your dedication to public welfare and promotion of education has always been admired. If you can establish a vocational school based on your own industry or make an existing school vocationalized, it will directly benefit the supply of talent and the development of your industry. At the same time, it will have a very good impact on society. For the sake of the development of your industry, for the sake of alleviating unemployment, and for the sake of the national economy, it seems that such an organization is necessary. We believe that you gentlemen, with your foresight and leadership, will agree with this proposal. If you promote it, we will see a great response. If you consult us on this issue, our society will do our best to contribute what we know." Upon receiving this letter, we find that the common problem of our country's industries is that when undertaking a business, there are no employees who have received sufficient training and knowledge to apply it, while the common problem of the education sector is that the talents cultivated are unable to meet the current needs. Therefore, students often feel difficulties in finding employment after graduation or even go astray. Although the China Vocational Education Society was established to reverse this decline, the people in charge of the society are mostly from the education sector, so they are inevitably separated from the industry, failing to fully exert their effectiveness. The society's proposal to establish specialized vocational schools according to their needs is to make up for this shortcoming. Therefore, we have sent a special letter to inform you, hoping that your association will convene the industry to discuss this matter at length and make appropriate arrangements. If you sincerely promote it and achieve success, the livelihood problem that causes social panic can at least be partially solved. Please do not regard it as ordinary."
